Recent Situation of the Student Unrest in Six Counties of Anhui Province 174

The previous report mentioned the dispute between the school board and the principal of the Anhui Six Counties Middle School. According to confirmed information from Anhui, Principal Zou Song submitted his resignation to the Department of Education after the unrest occurred on the first day, which was promptly approved. The Department of Education also instructed the school board to form a committee to maintain school affairs temporarily until the new principal takes office. The committee elected Yang Huicun, Zhang Guoqiao, Duan Xizhi, Xu Bojiao, Wang Xueqiao, and Zhang Jieqing as members to oversee the transition. All teachers, except for a few who voluntarily resigned, continued in their positions, and classes resumed as usual the following day. It is also reported that the school board plans to nominate a new principal to the Department of Education for approval in the near future.

Lin Kanghou Talks About

Education Funding in Concessions 177

Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Lin Kanghou, the Chinese member of the Public Concession’s Works Department, at the Banking Association, inquiring about matters such as the Works Department’s requests for subsidies for educational expenses for schools established by Chinese people within the concession. According to the discussion, the Works Department allocates more than 150,000 taels annually to subsidize educational expenses within the concession, and there is currently no possibility of increasing this amount. Chinese schools within the concession can receive a strong 50% of this subsidy. Schools established by Chinese people within the concession that wish to request subsidies must have their applications transferred through the Municipal Bureau of Education. However, the Works Department has specific regulations regarding the issuance of subsidies to these schools, limiting them to matters such as adding new school buildings to meet school hygiene requirements. Requests that have not been approved recently are due to non-compliance with the aforementioned regulations. Rumors that the Works Department will increase this subsidy are not true.

A Comparative View of Records 190

▲Holds the National Record for 3000 Meters

▲Once Produced Two East China Records

▲Previous Scores All Surpassed Those of Universities

▲Still Two Records Better Than Jiangnan University's

Since its establishment, the Secondary School Sports Federation has held three track and field competitions. In terms of history, the period is very short. In terms of results, it is quite impressive. In the past, every time there was a middle school competition, its records were not only the best among the middle schools at the time, but also far surpassed the results of university sports. The facts are all there and can be verified. Anyone who knows a little about the sports situation in Shanghai can say this. Among them, the results of the second sports meeting in the 18th year of the Republic of China were the best. Among the 17 track and field events, 11 broke the records of the first meeting. Chen Xingpei's 3000 meters still holds the national record. Others, such as Wang Jihuai's triple jump and Chen Xingpei's 1500 meters, were also the highest records in East China at the time. Among these 11 new records, eight of the scores were not reached in the university sports and Shanghai open sports meeting of that year. The excellence of the scores was the best at the time. To this day, the scores of 200 meters and 1500 meters are higher than the highest records of universities. The scores of 400 meters, triple jump, javelin, and other three items are still better than the scores of this year's Jiangnan University Sports Meeting. All of these are the most glorious achievements of Shanghai middle school athletes in the history of sports, and are worthy of commemoration and admiration, and also worthy of being praised in front of the public. Looking back on the past and present, athletes from all schools should work harder to promote the glory of the association in the past. There are high expectations for today's meeting. (Xiang Qian)

A Brief History of the Secondary School Sports Federation 191

The association was established in the winter of the 16th year of the Republic of China. Counting the days, it has been six years since then. It aims to promote the development of sports and the cultivation of spirit in Shanghai's secondary schools. In the midst of connecting feelings, it cultivates the noble demeanor of athletes. Over the years, it has held various sports competitions, which have continued to this day. Initially, there were 12 basic member schools. Later, Lida Academy, Chengzhong Middle School, and Zhonghua Vocational Changshi Middle School withdrew one after another for various reasons, leaving eight schools. Later, Hujiang High School Affiliated to Nanyang Business College joined as new members, and finally Daxia High School Affiliated also joined, making a total of 11 member schools. Looking back at that time, the association was established after the Jiangnan University Sports Association in the large city of Shanghai. All the rules and regulations were based on the assistance of sports pioneers and the generous support of the authorities of various schools. The concerted efforts and mutual assistance of the members, with one heart and one mind, are the common creed that the association has adhered to over the years. On the occasion of the opening of the fourth track and field meeting, I would like to inform all sectors of society of what I know, and hope that people from all walks of life, sports pioneers, and the authorities of various schools will uphold their original intentions and encourage the younger generation, so that this fledgling infant can be nurtured into a child and grow day by day. It would be fortunate. (Lu Xiangqian)

Inter-Departmental Football Match Between Newspapers Yesterday

Shishi Wins Over Minbao 192

▲Result: Four to Two

丨Morning Post vs. Times Post Match Suspended Due to Rain丨

Shanghai's inter-departmental football match between newspapers, a pioneering event in China's journalism world, held its third and fourth matches yesterday afternoon at the Shanghai Municipal First Public Sports Field. At 4:00 PM, it was the Morning Post against the Times Post, and at 5:00 PM, it was the Shishi News against the Minbao. Details are listed below to record the grand occasion:

Morning Post vs. Times Post Match Suspended Due to Rain 193

As the clock struck four, thunder and rain began. The football field was already wet. The warriors from the Morning Post and the Times Post gathered inside the camp, rubbing their fists and preparing to fight. Yao Sufeng was in a bad mood and shouted "Let's compete!" The crowd responded. Therefore, captains Qu Yue and Jiang Zongdao decided to declare war and led their teams onto the field. Referee Zhang Longhai blew the whistle, and the scribes who usually bury their heads in writing suddenly showed the power of killing enemies on horseback. However, the weather was not good, with dark clouds gathering and heavy rain pouring down. The referee blew the whistle to retreat. After ten minutes, the clouds dispersed and the rain stopped, and the warriors returned to the field. But then a downpour fell again, so both sides agreed to temporarily suspend the war and decide the winner at 4:00 PM on the 26th.

Shishi Wins Over Minbao Four to Two 194

Showers continued until 5:30 PM. The warriors from Shishi News and Minbao were eager to try. Jiang Xiangqing first took off his shoes to demonstrate, and the others did not want to be left behind, so they changed clothes, took off their shoes, and rushed onto the field, their courage reaching the sky.

▲Muddy Figures　When Zhang Longhai gave the serious order to attack, Shishi News took the offensive first. Right wing Nie Shiqi got the ball and passed it to the center. The barefoot immortal Jiang Xiangqing shot but missed. Enraged, he fought bravely. The water and mud were slippery, making it difficult to keep his feet. He chased after the ball, clearly distinguishing himself. Afterwards, there was a continuous sound of slapping and falling on both sides. It is unknown how many people temporarily dressed up as muddy figures. Those who were careful to avoid falling were quite amusing to watch as they walked gracefully.

▲Wu Dong Saves the Day　After ten minutes of fighting, Shishi News gained a free kick opportunity in the chaos, about fifteen yards from the enemy's goal. Jiang Xiangqing kicked it barefoot, hitting it squarely. Minbao goalkeeper Wu Dong caught it and threw it out, overcoming the difficulty.

▲Shishi Wins Again　But in a blink of an eye, Shishi's iron cavalry rushed through two lines of defense. Right wing Nie Shiqi dribbled the ball to the center. Jiang Xiangqing got the ball, stood firm, aimed, and shot. The ball went into the net, opening the scoring. After restarting, before the formation was stable, Shishi's advance troops arrived in Minbao's territory again, and Nie Shiqi kicked in another goal.

▲Minbao's Misfortune　After several scrambles, Minbao made some progress and was about to launch a direct attack when they were penalized for a handball, about twenty-five yards from the goal. Jiang Xiangqing volunteered again, kicking the ball hard. Wu Dong calmly saved the day a second time. However, one wave had not subsided before another rose. Shishi's three armies surged forward, and Jiang Xiangqing took advantage of the opportunity to shoot from an oblique angle. Wu Dong moved to meet it, slipped, and fell to the ground, losing another goal, which was truly unfortunate. This was the situation in the first half.

▲Goalkeeper Slips　In the second half, the formations of both sides changed slightly. On the Shishi side, Jiang Xiangqing retreated to be the goalkeeper, and Xia Kaiming went to the front line to attack. On the Minbao side, Wu Dong also moved to the left wing to lead the front line, turning defense into offense, full of ambition. No sooner said than done, the muddy ball flew up and went straight to the Shishi News's net. Jiang Xiangqing caught it and was about to shoot when the enemy cavalry arrived, skillfully dodging around and losing his balance, falling backwards into the net, losing a goal.

▲Old Immortal Saves the Day　After restarting, Shishi's advance troops took the opportunity to attack again, and Gong Zhongxian from the left wing got a ball. But the Minbao team was determined not to give up, trapping Jiang Xiangqing in a situation where he was surrounded on all sides. Fortunately, the old immortal Pan Gongbi arrived alone on horseback and cleared the ball with one kick.

▲Last Touch of Glory　However, the Minbao team's attack became more urgent from then on. After several twists and turns, Zhang Zhen from the right wing finally scored a goal, creating a score of two to four. Although Minbao lost, its strength should not be ignored.

Special Feature

Overview of Education in Various European Countries (II) 198

— Recorded by Lu Bingqian

(I) England and France. There have not been many changes in British education after the war. Originally, the British national character valued freedom and disliked restrictions. We only need to look at the fact that their laws are unwritten, and even their constitution is so, but the British can consciously abide by them, believing that abiding by the law is not for the sake of the law, but a duty that should be fulfilled. Moreover, the British like to stick to the old ways. For anything, even if they know it is bad, they would rather let it develop gradually than use drastic reforms. Therefore, new ideas are not accepted in England. This situation is different from that of the United States. British education has no system. Their Ministry of Education is run by private individuals, and everyone does things according to their own will, without government intervention, resulting in uneven quality. However, after the war, they were able to recognize their mistakes and adopted two methods to remedy this problem. First, they implemented a unified examination system to check the academic achievements of various schools. A group of schools, in order to maintain their position and reputation in society, participated in the unified examination, so they could be brought into line imperceptibly. Second, they stipulated a subsidy system. Many schools with insufficient resources could enjoy subsidies. To enjoy subsidies, they must first comply with the conditions promulgated by the government, so the schools could be brought together imperceptibly. This compromise and reconciliation method is very suitable for the British national character. As for major reforms, they did exist at the beginning of the European War, with people drafting education reform plans, wanting to thoroughly transform the schools. This kind of major reform was originally not very suitable for the British national character, but later, when the war had just ended and everyone was mentally exhausted, even though everyone knew it was unsuitable, they were powerless to object. Therefore, it was passed in Parliament. However, in the end, only two or three tenths of it was implemented. The reason for this was, of course, economic difficulties, but also because of their inherent nature, they were determined not to use revolutionary means to reform the system and methods of education. Seeing this point, the Ministry of Education organized many committees in 1926, such as those for primary schools, secondary schools, and universities, to gradually promote based on national character. Therefore, there have not been many changes in British education after the war. France is also similar. French education is systematic and is all regulated by the government. Even the specific pages to be taught in a certain lesson at a certain time are all regulated. After the war, there were slight changes, and the facilities of the schools could be used for free activities, but there were very few opportunities. France was the earliest to have a revolution, but the concept of class is very deep. The admission of the upper class and the lower class is different. The upper class can enter preparatory schools, from middle school to university. The lower class can only enter ordinary schools and have no opportunity to enter middle school or university. Therefore, their school system can be called a dual-track system. After the war, a group of influential people advocated reform and unification, determined only by each person's ability.

(II) Emerging Countries. They have no education system at all. After the establishment of the country, they strive to create a new system, but due to insufficient financial resources, they can only try economic methods. The plan they have set is based on the distribution of the local population. First, they investigate which place has the densest population and which place has the sparsest population. What is the distribution of the population in villages and cities? How far is the distance between villages and cities? Then they compile statistics to decide which places should establish schools. All school-age children within ten kilometers (approximately ten li) of all schools can enter nearby schools. In this way, the schools will not be duplicated, nor will there be a lack. The same is true for primary schools and secondary schools. This plan is really an economic method, but it can also achieve great results.

(III) Germany and Austria. They used to be autocratic countries. The educational goal was not for individuals, but for the imperial system. After the war, the political direction changed, and new education also rose. Therefore, new education laws are easily seen in Germany and Austria, especially in Germany, where many new schools have been established. When we talk about education, it seems that the United States is indispensable, but in reality, the educational methods and achievements of Germany and Austria are very admirable and can be emulated.

(IV) Russia and Italy. They regard education as a political tool, so the changes are also very large.

III. European Education Trends. Summarizing the recent trends in education in various European countries, (I) before the war, education in various countries had no major goals. After the war, various countries saw national decline and improper education, so they decided on education policies and then acted according to the policies. The content of the policies, simply speaking, is to make education available to all, so that everyone has the opportunity to enjoy education. In the past, educational rights in France were very unequal, and some people were often restricted. Their abilities were worthy of being enjoyed, but they were not allowed by law. Now, the so-called dual-track system and multi-track system have all been broken, and they are exploring new paths there. (II) Emphasizing National Defense. European countries implement education and extremely emphasize national defense education. Their teaching materials and teaching methods are all like this. For example, the glorious history of the country, etc., are all considered good materials, so that all children can understand them in their hearts. Especially for emerging countries, with an unstable foundation, it is necessary to make children have patriotic thoughts and concepts, so attention must be paid to education. (III) Production-oriented, that is, vocational. They do not advocate cultivating a group of unemployed idlers. They want to enable everyone to have considerable vocational skills after receiving education. Moreover, education should not be limited to schools. Schools can only represent a small part of education and cannot represent the entirety of education. Education outside of schools has the same value. The so-called social education is strongly advocated by them because it can equally enlighten the public, especially in Russia. In educational administration, it does not take schools as units, but divides educational undertakings into social education, vocational education, political education, etc. Political education does not necessarily run primary schools or secondary schools or universities. This method is very worthy of our attention. China takes schools too seriously, thinking that running schools is all that is needed to run education. This is wrong. (IV) Regarding the life of teachers, all countries are very miserable. Like the teachers in Poland and England, the work is very heavy. In the past, they taught 22 lessons per week, but now they have to teach 30 lessons, and some even have their salaries reduced, so their lives are very poor. Moreover, like the school buildings in our country and Poland, they are also very simple, but their spirit is very good.

Free Talk

Heaven and Earth 199

— Gan

China now has two kinds of bombing, one is bombing in, and the other is bombing in. An example of bombing in is: "Except for the planes bombing the bandit areas, there were no battles during the day. Teams three and four flew from the 7th morning to Shen (Shanghai), taking turns in teams to fly west of Yihuang and south of Chongren, dropping two to three hundred 120-pound bombs. All the places where the bandits could use as cover were bombed and destroyed almost completely, so that the bandits had no place to rest..." (Shenbao Nanchang Special Dispatch, May 10)

An example of bombing in is: "At six o'clock this morning, enemy planes bombed Jixian County, killing more than ten civilians. In addition, Miyun County was bombed four times by the enemy, with two planes each time, dropping over a hundred bombs. The damage is being investigated..." (Datong Evening News Beijing Dispatch on the same day)

Born out of this "movement" are the Shanghai elementary school students buying airplanes and the Beijing elementary school students digging caves.

This is also a good article on the topics of "No internal pacification, no external resistance" or "Internal pacification is more urgent than external resistance."

People living in the concessions are blessed. But if you close your eyes and think about it more broadly, you will feel that the inside is the government soldiers in the sky, and the "Communist bandits" and the "banditized" people are on the ground; the outside is the enemy army in the sky, and the non-"banditized" people are on the ground. "The damage is being investigated," while in the peaceful area, a pagoda is being built. When Shakyamuni was born, he pointed one finger to the sky and one finger to the ground, saying: "Above and below the heavens, I alone am honored!" This is what it means.

But if you close your eyes and think about it for a longer time, you will encounter a difficult question. If the bombing in is slow and the bombing in is fast, what will happen when the two kinds of planes meet? Will they stop the "internal pacification" and turn around to "fight head-on," or will they still only take care of bombing in, letting the other follow along bombing in, one in front and one behind, bombing the "bandit areas" together, waiting until they are cleared, and then "resist" them out? ...

But this is just a joke. In fact, it will never come to this point. Even if it comes to this point, there is nothing difficult to solve: recuperating abroad, worshiping Buddha in famous mountains, and that's the end of it.

Three Years Later 200

— Luo Hong

He eagerly awaited tomorrow, tomorrow would bring him a different destiny. He watched his body, worn down by the time in prison, but he knew his heart was not broken.

There were so many injustices in the world; just because a friend he lived with had committed a crime, he was implicated and thrown into prison as well. He only knew this friend after they started living together, and he still didn't fully understand what crime the man had committed. Being arrested together wasn't really surprising; they lived in the same house and were about the same age, so it was easy to become a suspect. Once in prison, two lawyers defended his friend, but they shifted many of the pieces of evidence and facts onto him. Although he denied it and defended himself, it was useless. He didn't have money to hire a lawyer, and his parents back in his hometown didn't have the money to hire a lawyer for him either. Thus, he was convicted; but he didn't know what happened to the one who actually committed the crime. From that moment on, he suspected something behind the law, what the law was built upon.

He finally left the prison, where he had lived for three years, amidst the farewell glances of his companions. As soon as he stepped outside, the first thing he felt was the bright sunlight and fresh air; however, this light and freshness soon faded away, gradually dimming.

The streets were much busier than before. New buildings, resplendent, tall, the things in the display windows were truly dazzling. Women's dresses were long enough to cover their heels, and some were higher on the left and lower on the right, as if the tailor had cut them wrong, dragging along in varying lengths.

He forgot his hair, which had grown more than three inches long, forgot the dirty and wrinkled jacket he was wearing, only felt the emptiness in his stomach, and the emptiness in his heart. The world before him was too far removed from him.

He didn't know where the strength came from, but as he thought, his spirits perked up; the new horrors were like a whip lashing at his heart.

He walked on, oblivious to everything, because he had too many things to fear in his heart. In front of a large store, he saw a familiar face, and that person also looked at him. It was truly coincidental. Upon closer inspection, the familiar face was the friend he had lived with, the friend who had caused him to spend three years in prison. But his appearance was much more prosperous than before.

"Shafei, I didn't expect to see you today," the man said awkwardly first.

"Today marks three years, you haven't forgotten, have you?"

"Ah, yes, I'm sorry for what happened to you..."

"What exactly were you doing back then that got the authorities to arrest you and make me serve three years in prison for you?"

The friend replied embarrassedly, "At that time, I had many friends who organized an association to oppose the authorities. I participated in this while studying. Somehow, the matter was leaked, and you and I were arrested together that day, along with many others who were arrested. My family has wealthy uncles who hold official positions. I usually argued with my family because I opposed my own family. After that incident was exposed, my family used various methods to save me. With money and an uncle who was an official, things became easy to handle. At the time, I was very opposed, but the lawyer spoke for me, saying that I had a mental illness and wasn't allowed to speak..."

"So what are you doing now?..."

"Now, after being released by the court, I returned to the university where I was studying, graduated from the law department, and now I work in the Ministry of Justice..."

It turned out that the friend who had caused him to spend three years in prison had long been an official in the Ministry of Justice.

Did he hate him? No. It wasn't entirely his fault.

However, when this friend, with a hint of apology, invited him to his home, he didn't say anything, only cast a contemptuous glance at him, and turned away.

Funeral 201

— Lin Huiyin

A child, just over a month old, fell ill with pneumonia and was staying in the hospital. Judging from the situation that night, his journey seemed to be coming to an end; when I saw it, I thought that this might be the last glance, and told the people in the hospital: if anything happens, please call me. After saying that, I trudged home with a sorrowful gait.

The next morning, the phone rang, saying that the child had passed away from the pneumonia.

I packed a set of clothes that had been made but not yet worn, and emptied a suitcase, and brought it to the hospital. The child's body was still slightly warm, and his complexion had not changed much; I changed him into the clothes and placed him in the suitcase. I then took him to the burial site that had been pre-arranged.

When the car arrived at Wusong Town, I thought I had reached the seaside, so I got out of the car indifferently. After getting out of the car, I realized that there was still some distance to the seaside. Afraid that the rickshaw would be too bumpy, I carried the suitcase silently and walked slowly, from the bustling town to the stone embankment where there was hardly any trace of people.

The weather that day was no less dim than my mood, and there was also some wind, so the sound of the waves on the stone embankment accompanied me. When I reached the middle of the embankment, the wind seemed especially strong, and the waves were especially heavy. I thought the tide was coming in. The tide might flood this embankment, I thought again. I looked ahead, and then looked back. I didn't know how fast the tide would come in. The tide was indeed coming, and it was getting faster and faster. Could I still go forward? I hesitated in my heart, but my feet kept moving. So I looked back again, and saw that the distance between the shore and me was longer than the distance between me and the lighthouse. But it seemed to take some time to get to the lighthouse. Go back? I didn't want to. I looked at the suitcase. Although my heart was not as turbulent as the waves, it could be said that it was still very calm, and my pace was still moving at the original rate. I thought that this funeral might turn into a burial with the dead, but I didn't believe that such a thing would happen. I saw a boat parked not far away. This was the last time I was doing my best for him. I wanted to go forward, looking at the lighthouse.

Finally, I reached the end of the stone embankment. I opened the suitcase and threw him into the sea. I stared at him, undulating with the waves. As if knowing my thoughts, he kept rolling outward, never lingering, getting smaller and smaller, and finally, so small that it was beyond my sight. So my heart seemed to loosen, thinking that he had escaped this earthly world, had escaped my heart.

This is how I sent off the child's funeral, the child that had worried me for more than a month.

Random Jottings from the Cottage 202

— Yu Zhan

(Twenty-nine) National Martial Arts and Foreign Insults

Mr. Zhigang saw my article "National Martial Arts and Foreign Insults" and showed me a passage from the "Lin Ju Man Lu" (Random Records from a Cottage) by Wu Yuanhua of the Ming Dynasty, which he had recorded in his manual. Only then did I learn that using national martial arts to resist Japan had existed since the Ming Dynasty. Moreover, that person was the Provincial Governor of Shandong, which is equivalent to the position of the current Shandong Chairman. One ancient and one modern, echoing each other from afar, is absolutely interesting and must be recorded. "Lin Ju Man Lu" says: "Song Gong of Tongjiang had eloquence and a great love for numerology. When he was Provincial Governor of Shandong, Japanese pirates invaded Korea, and alarm bells rang everywhere. Gong ordered the prefectures of Dengzhou and Laizhou to collect tens of thousands of chicken eggs each. When asked what they were for, he said, 'The Japanese come by boat, and I will throw chicken eggs at them. The boat will be slippery, and they won't be able to stand, and we will capture them all.' Those near and far all laughed, but only Lanxi admired him, promoted him to Junior Sima, and appointed him as the General Superintendent of military affairs to conquer the Japanese. Earlier, there was a Taoist named Zhang Junjiu who possessed minor magic tricks. Gong invited him to be a guest in his tent. Once he arrived in Liaodong, he demanded two hundred tables from the people, stacked several feet high. Junjiu let down his hair, held a sword, stood on the table, and shouted to the crowd, 'In three days, there will be a hundred thousand heavenly soldiers to help me destroy the Japanese.' The next night, he secretly went to a brothel to stay and fought with a military officer, injured his eye, and fled. Gong was greatly disappointed and falsely said, 'I have even more magical arts, and I will make the Japanese chieftains tie themselves up and surrender to me.' Alas! Even if the imperial court lacks talent, why should it appoint a verbose and strange person to be in charge of one side, desecrate the prestige of China, and invite the contempt of the barbarians?" In the past few days, Shandong Province is holding a national martial arts examination, having already recruited extraordinary talents who can fly over eaves and walk on walls and use acupressure. They should also obtain knights who can swallow knives, spit fire, and fly swords. It is hoped that in the future, when resisting Japan, they will quickly achieve skin-deep results. These wandering knights of the martial arts world should be declared to the national history and biographies, and novelists will no longer have to make empty lies! Wouldn't that be great?

Red Carrot Whiskers 203

— Jules Kenaru, translation adapted by Lin Quzuo

The Blind Man (continued)

But Lépiek's wife was using a clever trick. She brushed against the blind man, she bumped him with her elbow, she stepped on his foot, she made him retreat, forcing him to sit between the cupboard and the wardrobe, in the unheated area. The blind man was disoriented, groping, making gestures, his fingers clinging like animals. He was making a commotion in the dark. The ice in his veins had congealed again, and now he was freezing to death.

The blind man finished his story in a voice that sounded like he was about to cry.

"Yes, my good friends, it's over, no eyes, nothing, just pitch black."

He accidentally knocked over his cane. This was exactly what Lépiek's wife was waiting for. She hurriedly ran over, picked up the cane, and returned it to the blind man, but she didn't actually return it to him.

He thought he had received it, but he hadn't.

She was deceiving him so cleverly, and then she made him change his seat. She gave him his clogs and led him towards the door.

Then she gently pinched him, just to vent her anger; she pushed him out the door, pushed him under the snowy, gloomy sky, pushed him into the howling wind.

Before closing the door, Lépiek's wife shouted desperately at the blind man, as if dealing with a deaf person:

"Goodbye; don't lose the money; if the weather is good and you are still alive, see you next Sunday. Really! You're right, old man Dixier, we'll never know whether we'll die or live tomorrow. Everyone has their troubles, and God treats everyone the same!"

New Year's Day

It was snowing. In order to make New Year's Day a New Year's Day, it should of course snow.

Lépiek's wife had thoughtfully bolted the courtyard gate the night before. Early in the morning, many naughty children ran over and shook the bolt. Everyone crowded outside the gate. At first they were polite, but then they got angry and kicked it with their clogs. Finally, they were too lazy to wait any longer and retreated, but they still turned back to look at Lépiek's wife, who was hiding there peeking at them through the window. The sound of their footsteps disappeared in the snow.

Red Carrot Whiskers jumped out of bed and ran to the sink in the garden to wash his face. But there was no soap. The sink was already frozen. He had to break the ice. This early exercise made him feel hot all over, which was really more beneficial than a stove. But he only wet his face a little and didn't wash it clean, so others often thought he was dirty. Even if he immersed his face in the water to wash it, he would only remove the most obvious dirt.

He briskly and freshly participated in the New Year's greetings. He stood behind his older brother Felix, and Felix stood behind his older sister Elestine. The three children walked into the kitchen together. Lépiek and Lépiek's wife were already waiting there, both looking like nothing was amiss.

Sister Elestine embraced and kissed them and said:

"Good morning, Dad. Good morning, Mom. I wish you a happy New Year, good health, and ascent to heaven in the future."

Older brother Felix said the same, speaking fluently and extremely quickly, and also embraced and kissed them.

But Red Carrot Whiskers was different. He took out a letter from his hat. The tightly sealed envelope was written with: "Presented to my parents." The envelope did not have a place name written on it. In the corner of the envelope was a magnificent bird with splendid feathers, in the act of flapping its wings and flying.

Red Carrot Whiskers handed the letter to Lépiek's wife, and she opened the letter. The stationery was decorated with several blooming flowers, and a circle of lace was sewn around the stationery. When Red Carrot Whiskers wrote, he often dropped the pen into the eyelets of the lace, and even ruined the words near the lace.

Lépiek: What about me, don't I get anything!

Red Carrot Whiskers: This is for both of you; Mom will pass it on to you.

Lépiek: In this way, you favor your mother. Well, search your body and see if that new six-sou coin is in your pocket! (To be continued)

Securities: Delivery Approaching, Bond Market Short Squeeze 210

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange experienced a sudden short squeeze in public bonds. Shorts began to panic. The US President issued a telegram ensuring world peace, and Huang Fu arrived in Tianjin, further solidifying the atmosphere of peace. Market sentiment was exceptionally strong. However, given the magnitude of these events, they are not to be taken lightly. The short squeeze is due to the approaching delivery date, creating a bullish trend with signs of prosperity. At the opening yesterday morning, only Reorganization bonds No. 21 and No. 43 were sold slightly, dropping a fraction of a cent and a half. Starting with forward-dated Reorganization bonds, buying pressure was strong, gradually pushing prices higher. Subsequently, various bonds saw even more significant gains, some rising by as much as sixty cents. In the second session, short sellers were increasingly covering their positions. Apart from forward-dated Consolidated Tax bonds which fell slightly by a cent, the rest continued to rise by thirty to fifty cents, indicating a clear short squeeze. In the afternoon session, there was back and forth trading between bulls and bears. Bonds rose by thirty to fifty cents and fell by twenty to thirty cents. When the forward-dated Salt Tax bond was auctioned, number 32 experienced a surge in selling, and the market price dropped from high to low, only ending up five cents higher. This caused a sudden change in the situation. At the close, the market was uncertain. Initially, various bonds rose or fell only twenty to thirty cents. However, when Salt Tax was auctioned, number 46 suddenly experienced a large sell-off, causing a dramatic shift in trend. The market price plummeted by one dollar and twenty cents, and forward-dated bonds also fell by ninety cents. This was also a result of prices being too high, attracting large-scale selling. As a result, only Salt Tax fell by twenty to thirty cents, while the rest continued to rise from twelve cents to one dollar. The total trading volume amounted to 17,244,200 yuan, of which 19,200 yuan was in spot contracts, and futures contracts for Consolidated Salt Tax, Troop Reduction, 1920 Customs, and 2020 Customs accounted for 7,525,000 yuan, 2,490,000 yuan, 2,465,000 yuan, and 3,615,000 yuan respectively, while the rest ranged from tens of thousands to two hundred thousand yuan.

Silk and Tea: Recent News on Sericulture in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

Dantu 219

The early silkworms in the four rural districts have already entered the "grand sleep" with lush leaves. The next batch are also waking up from their "grand sleep," and the late batch are also feeding on leaves during their third instar. This year, the weather is sunny and warm, and many silkworm farmers are raising foreign breeds, with supervisors assisting them. The silkworm eggs are developing well, and the leaf production is high, with leaf prices also low. However, in recent days, thunderstorms have repeatedly occurred, with strong winds, rain, and hail, causing the early silkworms in the Yaojiaqiao area to undergo changes, with diarrhea and delayed sleep. The late silkworms' sleep is also uneven. Supervisors are rushing to rescue them, isolating the diseased silkworms. In another week, the early silkworms will show new promise.

Hang County 220

The improved breeds raised in the Gao Si and Sanbao areas of Linping are not few. Supervisors are guiding the rearing with new methods, and the silkworm eggs are developing smoothly. The early batch has entered the "grand sleep," the next batch is also feeding on lush leaves during their third instar, and the late batch is also feeding on enough leaves during their second instar. In recent days, thunderstorms have been hot and humid, causing the early silkworms to eat leaves sluggishly and delay their sleep. Supervisors are currently trying to take care of them, and the losses are still small. However, the remaining local breeds in the four rural districts are now producing lush leaves, but silkworm farmers are not careful in feeding the leaves, and the silkworms are eating rainwater-soaked leaves, occasionally showing symptoms such as yellow diarrhea and black vomiting. Farmers and silkworm farmers alike are worried. Less than 50% of the silkworm houses in the four rural districts have been rented out.

Talk

Talking about "Dragon Boat Festival", "Dragon Boat Racing", "Strike" and "Resisting Insults", etc. 233

— Xiao Zhi

The "lunar calendar" has been abolished, and although many people say that they have gradually become accustomed to the "solar calendar." However, friends who "eat fast and chant Buddha" still firmly remember "the first day" and "the fifteenth day": filial sons and virtuous grandchildren who understand "wooden roots and water sources" and deeply remember their ancestors have not given up "Qingming" and "Zhongyuan." As for "Mid-Autumn Festival", "Dragon Boat Festival", "Lantern Festival" and the like, they are even more of a good time and festival that children and the general public are most willing and eager to arrive. I heard the old lady Wang next door say that the "Dragon Boat Festival" of "Gui You Year" is coming. She has already told her daughters-in-law to prepare the best "realgar" and "wormwood", and is rushing to make festive decorations such as "Dragon Boat Festival rope." According to A-Gen, her family's chauffeur, "The Dragon Boat Festival is really lively in the countryside, with dragon boat races and lantern shows!" Yes, yesterday's newspaper also told us that Jiading County, which has not had "dragon boat races" for many years, also has people initiating them this year. Dongmenwai, Nanmen Shigangmen, Ximenwai Gang, Beimen Loutang and other places have all held this grand event; however, unfortunately, when the enthusiastic members of the urban area were "holding books and stamping on various stores to launch the lantern show", they were spotted by the police captain of the county, and two people were immediately arrested, causing a police-civilian conflict, with dozens of people beaten to a bloody pulp! And the situation escalated, "the whole city went on strike! (See this newspaper on the 15th of this month for details)

Speaking of "strike", I can't help but think of the large-scale city-wide strike in Shanghai after "January 28th" (but I don't know if Jiading City also went on strike at that time? Because no one from Jiading has told me); speaking of "Jiading City", I also think of the Japanese planes that flew over their city last year to show off their power, and the bombs of one hundred and dozens of pounds also visited this "happy" land. The people of Jiading saw these things and were so frightened that their faces turned pale and they hid in the houses or cellars (but I don't know if these things still leave some vague shadows in the minds of the people of Jiading?) However, it is said that the strike in Shanghai last year was "resisting insults", and this strike in Jiading City, I think, is probably also "resisting insults." However, Shanghai is resisting insults because the Easterners want to occupy Zhabei, and Jiading City is resisting the insult of the police force because the dragon boat race cannot be held, which is slightly different. However, therefore, someone is asking: Why do you say that the people of Jiading City are striking to resist insults? Well, please listen to me:

(1) Because "dragon boat racing" is an inherent national essence of China. Preserving this national essence is as important as preserving antiquities and excavating ancient tombs;

(2) Because "dragon boat racing" is a happy act and also has a bit of celebration. Since the Eastern Xiaochilao did not bomb Jiading City like Zhabei in Shanghai last year, isn't this happy and worth celebrating enough?

(3) Although it is said that North China is in extreme danger now, fortunately, there are the mysterious predictions of the "sage" committee members of "the revolution will inevitably rise in that country in three years" and "waiting for fifty years", so we Jiading City is not Beiping City now, why don't we enjoy it?

(4) Sutras can save the country, dancing can also save the country, so of course "dragon boat racing" can also save the country!

………for these reasons, the police force did not know or understand these profound theories and dared to arbitrarily arrest reasonable people to the point of two people, isn't this a complete insult to the people of Jiading City? The people of Jiading City beat the police to a bloody pulp, and even evolved into a "city-wide strike". This is of course the most effective means of "resisting insults"…………

What's more, the fifth old lady next door to my house also said, "The police force is too unreasonable and should not be!"

News Brought by the Spring Breeze 234

— Ping

Friend, the spring break has long passed, and spring has quietly returned. I, who am busy with life, can leisurely sit on the Jinghu train. The reason is very simple. We poor people are not qualified to have travel interests. Sitting on the Jinghu train is still for the sake of life. Friend, do you know that I have recently OUt of Uob again in Shanghai?

Last year, you returned from the capital and said, "Places like the Confucius Temple are full of ugliness, and they try their best to interrogate young couples in hostels. This is the trick of our great country!" Friend, Zhenjiang is the same place.

After dinner with friends, a group of people stepped into Zhenjiang's only big hotel, Dahua Hotel. Although it also has facilities such as bathrooms, it is still below Central Shenzhou in comparison.

"Are there any flower girls here?" C joked in Shanghai-style Zhenjiang dialect:

"Are there flower girls?" The bellboy replied, "You can't come to the warehouse. If the room inspector finds out, they will be arrested." We all laughed at his fluent Zhenjiang dialect. C laughed even more: "Flower girls are probably not as fun as this bellboy!" After saying that, everyone laughed wildly again. The bellboy couldn't understand what we were saying and laughed inexplicably.

Of course, we couldn't go anywhere to play that day, but we couldn't fall asleep after only nine o'clock. My friend said, "Let's go to the red light district. I'll take you somewhere to play."

"Sir, you're from Zhenjiang!" The bellboy thought we were all from Shanghai. Hearing my friend's local language, he asked in surprise, "Then the gentleman will take you to the back street to play."

But my Zhenjiang friend was still acquainted in Shanghai. He goes home for a month every spring break. He knows where the back street is: he doesn't know where the girls in the back street are.

We arrived at Baota Lin, which is a public singing venue, with the same equipment as the former Great World Qunfang Hui singing hall. There is also a white-character water sign prohibiting strange noises, which was ordered by the Public Security Bureau. When the flower girls sang, their flirtatious eyes flew around. Perhaps knowing that we were from Shanghai, they especially posed.

A middle-aged man who looked like a smoker leaned over from behind me and whispered, "Old man, would you like to order a song?"

I asked my friend what the rules were. He said that was a pimp. If you take a fancy to a girl, order a few plays for her. Each play costs one yuan, and you can go to her house after the show. Friend, is the Confucius Temple probably the same kind of place?

Stepping out of Baota Lin, my friend met a veteran in the flowers and asked him to take us to the back street to play. The back street is a belt of small alleys, like the alleyways of Shanghai, but there are no signs like red lights. You can't ask for directions without acquaintances. With the permission of that gentleman, we sat down in a house called Something Lan. Because it was Saturday, many masters from the XX Bureau and Hall were there drinking and gambling. The patrol police outside were like nothing had happened. According to that gentleman, our Special Generation is not the era where colleagues were killed. It was because of exposing this kind of trick.

I hope this letter will not be checked, otherwise Shanghai will have to hold a big meeting again. I have already set the itinerary for tonight, and will return to Shanghai in at most five days. I have bought half a dozen Zhenjiang vinegar as a gift for your wife. (To be continued)

Literary and Artistic

Ode to a Vase 235

— Shen Min

Jade standing tall, both glamorous and delicate,

Its gentle and charming state is hard to depict,

Fluffy and stylish, in a Western fashion,

Graceful waist, like willow branches,

Exquisitely small and endearing,

It brings spring into the room, a legendary tale,

Ridiculous are the crazy bees and lustful butterflies,

Picking flowers and flirting, so entangled,

Bright reds and purples competing with the flowers,

Same beauty, different makeup,

The vase is outstanding, the place blessed, business thriving,

The blooming flowers, understanding speech, revealing the spring light,

Equality between men and women is praiseworthy,

A free flower is offered high on the desk,

Men should lose some of their dominance,

Fashionable and modern, even flesh is numb.

An Interview with a Nanny 236

— Li Shu

"Foreign goods are better than domestic goods." A chubby, blonde-haired child was standing lively on the ground in the park, stumbling and falling as she imitated running, babbling in her heavenly language to the nanny sitting on the chair. Out of curiosity, I walked over and picked her up. She smiled, her small eyes narrowing to a line. I kissed her, and she seemed shyly to avoid me, still uttering "Ba...Ba" sounds from her little mouth.

When she saw Chinese people, she would call them "Papa."

The nanny explained her intention to me.

"Her father is Chinese, right?" "Yes." Indeed, Chinese raw materials made into goods in foreign factories are exceptionally beautiful.

"Her parents must love her very much?"

"This little girl is with me. Her father loves her even more."

"How much do you earn a month?"

"Including food, four dollars a month. I don't want to. It's still better in a local family."

"What? Isn't it the same as a Chinese family?"

"Humph! Her mother is really annoying. She's unclear about things and nags endlessly, and there are so many trivial matters."

"What about her father?"

"He works in a foreign firm. He's also afraid of her mother." She scolds him too, and sometimes he even has to kneel before her. Her father is very docile, it's really funny.

"They are happy!"

"Oh, too cheesy and unsightly. When they go out, they always kiss, and it's the same when they come back."

"This is Westernization."

"Alright, you say Westernization. She doesn't want us to speak Chinese. She says it's too stupid and doesn't sound good. Sometimes her father tells the little girl to speak Chinese, and she scolds him too!"

"Marrying a foreign wife, does he have to act like a foreigner too?" "No, her mother has a fortune. I heard he went to study in France relying on her."

Oh! I understand. I gave the little girl a kiss and went to stroll elsewhere.

Separated by a Single Wall 237

— Bai Tao

Life in Shanghai is truly interesting. A small shikumen house is home to as many as five or six families: one in the front building, one in the back building, one in the garret, one in the kitchen annex, one in the main room, and another in the loft. In total, there are dozens of people, big and small, men and women. However, despite living together, they never exchange a single word, as if they are determined to never interact with each other. Perhaps this is the source of the Shanghainese pride that makes them who they are.

My neighbor is separated from me only by a thin wall. Through the cracks in the wall, we can see each other. I have to walk past their door to enter or leave. Because the corridor is narrow, when we bump into each other, we press ourselves against the wall with our backs facing each other, as if we were strangers passing on the street. Only now do I understand the purpose of the wall; it seems that a single wall can separate you as if you were separated by a mountain!

My neighbor's dwelling is only about the size of two and a half eight-immortal tables. Yet, there are as many as eight people living inside. These people sleep inside like sardines in olive oil. Because summer has arrived, these sardines emit a stench that makes people afraid to approach.

I have no idea what noble occupation my neighbor engages in. They sleep during the day, although they also eat, but they sleep after eating. Nighttime is when they become active. The bedding is rolled up, and they immediately start playing mahjong with a clatter. The sounds of the tiles being shuffled, the loud shouts of "Pong!", the cries of calculating points,

Page 18

and the noisy arguments reverberate like thunder. They play until dawn, when they finally call it quits and fall asleep. My neighbor never cares about others. He is Chinese, and the world revolves around him. Therefore, under their noisy shouting, separated by a thin wall, I can only stare with wide eyes, lying in bed, being sacrificed by them. I am suffering from insomnia! Although I have told my neighbor to change to daytime, I don't have the authority to change their national character. However, when they are sleeping, even during the day, if someone makes noise, they will be subjected to his cursing of "your mother" and "pig."

The neighbor next door, as well as the neighbors upstairs and downstairs who are a bit further away, get up early in the morning and line up their chamber pots under the tap. After they "swish, swish, swish" for a while, they "whoosh" dump it out there. They spit everywhere, throw away cigarette butts, fruit peels, and paper scraps... No one interferes with any of this. These families live together, each for themselves. Although they may sweep their own little room, the public areas, such as the corridor, stairs, drying platform, and area around the tap, are never taken care of.

In the end, I had to move, leaving them to it. But wherever I moved, the situation was much the same.

Let's Reconcile! 238

The Confessions of a Nurse 239

— Fen

Many people constantly strive to seize every opportunity to tell others about their sufferings and grievances, hoping to gain people's sympathy. Although this is the dumbest thing to do, I am one of them. Now I want to tell you about everything about myself.

I believe what I write here is by no means my own abnormal state, but a sketch of the lives of nurses in general. Of course, this is what those gentlemen who care about social problems want to know.

I am an orphaned girl who lost her parents early in life and has not received people's love since childhood. I have no money, and I have no way to obtain higher education. Although I managed to graduate from a primary school, the education I received was very poor. Later, because there was no opportunity to make a living in the countryside, and I had to live, I had no choice but to follow an uncle to Shanghai to struggle as much as possible. The means of this struggle was to become a nurse.

When I mention the word nurse, I think you will think that their lives must be too romantic, especially if you are a man who has stayed in the hospital, then I guess accurately, you will immediately float up that kind of young and lively smile wearing a white cloth on your head. Perhaps this smile will never fade in your memory, but precisely because of this, our pain and sorrow will not be understood by people at all. In your eyes, we are bound to be prostitutes, or, to put it nicely, "great lovers" with many men.

Of course, this is not my own deliberate defilement, but in fact many vicious men have told me bluntly. At first, hearing such words, I was naturally angry and had to argue with him, but later I heard such words more and more, so I had to let them say it.

Why stop others from talking? In order to live, we have to work, we have to spend at least ten hours a day in the ward pouring chamber pots, making beds, feeding tea and rice, clearing bowels, and washing festering boils. And when the patient has a fever that is too high and goes mad, how can we violate the orders of the doctor and head nurse and not cater to them? Even holding a strange man and kissing is unavoidable. As for the bloody blood of the parturient women, it is enough to make people vomit. Other things like plugging the ears and mouths of the dead are also our daily meals. Although watching a person die in the dead of night cannot help but tremble.

Look! This is the life of me and our companions. Blood, corpses, urine, feces fatigue, fainting.

So, how should I comfort myself? There are many self-proclaimed virtuous men and women who explain it to us very nicely: "Love", "Mercy", "For God", "For saving the world", hum! Dog shit, get out, I have been anesthetized enough by you. And what I comfort myself with is that I have not starved to death until now.

So what am I hoping for? Where is our way out? In a word, I hope to use our own strength to improve our treatment, reduce working hours, follow the broad masses of toiling people, and move forward to create the world.

Store Clerk Communications

A Plea for Parents 241

Editor Sir:

I am a rice store accountant. Seven years ago, a neighbor introduced my second daughter to marry the only son of a Zhou family in the same village who owned some land. Since the Shanghai war broke out, after she saw him once, she often expressed her unwillingness to marry such an ugly tenant farmer as her husband. So I also deeply regretted it.

Today is the ninth day after their marriage. The first time she entered the room, she never wanted to sleep with her husband. She sat alone on the chair and cried all night: so they have no love between them. Now the other party has sent a matchmaker to say: if it continues like this, it will be resolved by law.

Sir, I am really in trouble. If I send someone to persuade her, she will not listen; if I say that it will be resolved by law, then it is related to face. Please give me a gospel! I wish you good health. Zhuang Liansheng respectfully

× × × ×

Editor's note: This matter, Zhuang Jun's current situation, is indeed extremely difficult. But thinking carefully, this kind of trouble is also brought by yourself. Your daughter, after all, has expressed her unwillingness to marry before, so you should explain to the other party and cancel the marriage contract. Fortunately, the law stipulates that "marriage contracts made by parents can be terminated if the children express their opposition after reaching adulthood." Even if there is some argument, it is much easier to handle than the current situation. Now, after hoping that persuading her to not change, there is only one way to listen to her divorce. However, even if a divorce can be obtained at present, the amount of compensation you have to pay to the other party will definitely be very considerable. The money they spent at the wedding must be compensated in full. If it is not handled well, you will have to pay a sum of money, which is called "consolation money" in law, as compensation for the other party's mental loss. This is a certain and inevitable result. You should still entrust the original matchmaker to discuss and discuss it to avoid getting involved in litigation and spending unnecessary money. If the negotiation is not settled, then you have to wait for the law to resolve it. As for face or no face, there is no need to worry too much about it.

Announcement for this column 242

This column aims to assist workers, shop assistants, apprentices, etc. in solving difficult problems. On the part of the letter writers, they should be satisfied with receiving a reply: In the past two months, thanks to the support of all sectors, there are more than ten sincere inquiries every day. Although we hold the aspiration of answering every letter; however, limited by facts, in addition to the problems that we believe are common to the general public, which are published daily in the newspaper, the remaining problems that are unique to individuals are answered directly by this column. However, in recent days, we have received many letters that have not clearly stated the address in accordance with the regulations. We guess their intention is nothing more than to hope that it will be published in the newspaper; and after carefully analyzing the content of the problems, it has nothing to do with the general public. If we follow the instructions to publish them one by one, not only will readers inevitably lose interest, but there is no space to accommodate the thirteen or fourteen letters received every day. We hope that future letters must be handled in accordance with the regulations in the simple rules of this column, especially the address must be clearly stated, otherwise we will not reply, please understand.

Simple rules for the store clerk communication column

(1) Purpose of communication: This column aims to gather ideas, explain difficult problems, learn from each other, and increase the happiness of life.

(2) Communication objects: The objects of this column are limited to shop assistants, apprentices, and workers in terms of people, and are based in this port in terms of location.

(3) Communication content: All about personal daily life such as:

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage, as well as other issues related to the country and society, are welcome. If the content of the problem is too deep and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be introduced to the "Reader Consultant" of this newspaper for answering.

(4) Method of letter writing

(1) The name, age, native place, occupation, and detailed mailing address must be written at the end of the letter; it must still be written when writing subsequent letters.

(2) The style of the letter is not limited, but it should be simple and easy to understand, and it must be written clearly.

(3) Please write the words "Store Clerk Communication Column, Supplementary Edition of Shen Bao Newspaper" on the envelope: if you need a reply, please attach two cents of postage.

(4) The correspondent must cut off the special stamp of this column and paste it in the upper left corner of the letter, if it is not pasted, we will not answer.

(5) Processing method after receiving the letter

(1) If this newspaper believes that the problem discussed has value in contributing to the public, it may be disclosed in the newspaper.

(2) In order to respect the opinions of the correspondents, if the letter states that they do not want their name to be disclosed, or if they need a separate reply, it can also be done.

(3) If the correspondent hopes that the letter will be disclosed in the newspaper, but because the length is too long and the full text cannot be disclosed, it should be published selectively. Also, if the content of the problem is complicated and has to be carefully studied, resulting in a delay in answering or disclosing it, please understand.

(4) In case of crowded letters, answers will be given in the order in which they were received, or there may be delays, please understand.

Novel

The Life of the Five Beauties (12) (Continued) 243

— Ling He

(11) The Best Years

Since Miss Liu was determined to live a new life, she moved from Beijing to Shanghai. The reason was very simple, because Beijing only had that dry air, which made her feel bored, which made her not have enough confidence to keep her youth. However, is this the only reason? This point, even those closest to her such as Wu Gui, could not understand, I am afraid only she herself would fully know.

But since Wu Gui followed Miss Liu to Shanghai, he always felt much more glorious than before. The most obvious thing was that he was already the official housekeeper, and such a rich family was actually a large mansion, and many nannies and servants had to be commanded by him. Of course, it was enough to be majestic.

Moreover, not only that, but everything in this house made him happy. For example, there was such a small garden outside the gate. In addition to roses in spring and chrysanthemums in autumn, he could also plant some balsams by hand in summer. However, Miss Liu was always not very fond of balsams, and she also disliked daffodils in winter, which he could not agree with Miss Liu. As for the furnishings in the house, he admired Miss Liu for being indeed capable. He didn't know where she bought so many exquisite furniture, such as that kind of strangely soft sofa, that kind of embroidered carpet, and those tea tables of different sizes. However, the arrangement method was completely different from Wu Gui's. He advocated placing a tea table between two grand master chairs, but she wanted to place the tea table crookedly next to the sofa, which was too irregular. As for placing a large bed in the middle of the house, it was also not very elegant. However, according to Miss Liu, this was the Western style. Although sleeping and eating did not necessarily have to be the same as Westerners, her own master must do so, and she deliberately learned it from other people's homes, perhaps all large mansions should be like this, so over time, she got used to it.

However, everything here was related to Miss Liu's position in the world, including that Italian breed of puppy specially selected for fifty silver dollars. For example, the guests who came here were all powerful bigwigs of today, and sometimes even foreigners wearing diamond pins on their ties would come to visit in cars. Therefore, the master's social circle was so wide that it was possible. Since this was the case, the equipment in the family had to be magnificent. As for having a puppy snuggled in her arms in the car, it seemed very appropriate, because not only foreign wives were like this, but Chinese gentlemen's wives had also learned this. Then Miss Liu was in fact the lover of gentlemen, so in every subtle action, she had to conform to the style of the wives, and things like bringing puppies were just basic conditions.

All in all, Miss Liu lived a very peaceful life for a long time, and Wu Gui could not help but feel relaxed when he thought of the scene back then.
