Movie Special

Joint Discussion of Peach Blossom Village and Spring River Flower Moon Night 244

— Shen Weng

A New Contribution After European Films Changed Their Style

A New Art of Melting Music and Film into One

European film production giant Eurik Pommer once said: "The duty of a film is to use entertainment to make people forget all worries, sorrows and unfortunate impressions. Nothing in the world can be as popular as a movie, because all mankind needs entertainment and craves entertainment. Therefore, entertainment films mixed with music are more popular; as for problem films, they can only win the welcome of a part of people in a limited social context." Whether what he said is right or wrong is another question. However, European films have recently changed their style under the influence of this argument, and the result has been successful.

We only need to look at the "Peach Blossom Village" Happy Ever After, which is now opening in Shaanxi, and the "Spring River Flower Moon Night" that has already been shown, are they not both using music to create poetic works? Then whether the audience welcomes it or not has already been proven by facts. Some people say that this kind of musical film is already a work of the past era in the United States. But you need to know that they are original and unique, and they infuse the harmonious art of music into the art of film. The American song and dance films that were popular a few years ago simply sent music to a dead end. They are completely different, which is because of good and bad use.

Speaking of the plot of these two films, they are certainly very simple: but they all carry some humorous mood in the simple. "Spring River Flower Moon Night" satirizes a group of philistines who blindly praise artists. The story of "Peach Blossom Village" satirizes European stars who only want to run to Hollywood. Indeed, as long as European stars on the screen or stage have a little reputation, they are immediately recruited by the United States. European filmmakers of course express dissatisfaction. But unfortunately, the heroine of "Peach Blossom Village," Lilin Howard, also finally went down this road. The magic power of money and vanity is indeed not small!

Speaking of skills, of course each has its own advantages. Photography and shooting in "Spring River Flower Moon Night" is pure art; while the photography of "Peach Blossom Village" uses some magic. The singing in "Spring River Flower Moon Night" is better than "Peach Blossom Village". But the expression of "Peach Blossom Village" is better than "Spring River Flower Moon Night" because they are all actors who can act. Furthermore, "Spring River Flower Moon Night" is completely a comedy, while "Peach Blossom Village" contains some bitterness in the laughter. Many places in the second half are full of sorrow. In short, these two films are no less than famous European works and are very worth appreciating.

Film Review

Review of "The Black Night Rope Shadow" 245

— Ming

The Black Night Rope Shadow (The Case of the Frightened Lady) – adapted from a novel into a stage play, and then from a stage play into a film. It is very famous in Europe and America. I remember that seven or eight years ago, there was an American silent film that was derived from this script, but the result was not as satisfactory as the stage play. This time it is produced by British Lion Film Corporation. It is really unexpected. America has been lively with horror films for a while, and Britain is actually using such a bizarre film to speculate.

The story is simply about a hereditary knight with a history of hereditary mental illness. When the disease occurs, he often kills people with a rope. Six people have been killed before and after. The police investigated the murderer, but found no clues. Soon, when the knight's old illness relapsed, he explained all the murders to the detective, and took out a pistol to prevent the detective from arresting him. Unexpectedly, when he moved his finger, he shot himself to death.

If you didn't know the story before watching the film, it would be difficult for you to guess who the murderer is, because the knight's mother is also highly suspected, and the two servants are also suspected of being murderers.

In terms of drama, the greatest contribution is maternal love. The knight's mother is an extremely shrewd and fierce woman, but she uses all kinds of methods to protect her son, and she also chooses a good daughter-in-law. On the one hand, she sees her capable skills, and on the other hand, she promotes great maternal love.

The director is not bad, and the structure is acceptable, but why does the girl pick up the rope when the detective goes to the knight's house to investigate? There is a room that the owner is not allowed to unlock. This loophole is lightly written in the film, but it is the director's fault. The light tends to be terrifyingly dark, which is quite suitable for the appropriate situation. Although there are few exterior scenes, they are all good. The interior scenes are really like those described in the original book, and they are also in line with the old residence of the knight. The photography is very novel, using a large number of overhead shots and仰攝, which is quite eye-catching, but unfortunately the "rope shadow" shots are too short and too few, which is slightly suspected of being slack.

Emlyn Williams, who plays the knight, only has the last monologue, which is the most exciting, with a painful and profound expression that is exceptionally moving. Cathleen Nesbilt, who plays the knight's mother, is also the best at the end. In the first half, she can only show a capable old woman, but she cannot show the attitude of a loving mother's hard work. The knight's fiancée is played by Belle Chrystall, who looks frightened everywhere. She provides the most horror colors for the whole film. The rest of the actors are the same as the above three protagonists, and their performances are ordinary, so there is no need to mention them.

In this film, there is no interlude to speak of. Originally, there is no need for interludes in this type of film, but a detective named Gordon Harker has some humorous words and actions, such as eating candy in the lecture hall, which are quite interesting.

As for the dialogue, like other British films, many funny places are contained in the dialogue.

I suspect that this is an old film from three years ago. Not only are the front-of-house staff lists and film titles not as new as in recent years, but the film also broke twice. However, whether it is a new product or an old product, it will not disappoint people anyway.

Review of "The Flower of Hell" 246

— Ling He

Simple Directing Technique

Excellent Performance by the Protagonist

In a realistic society where love is built on the foundation of money, this film "The Flower of Hell" (She Done Him Wrong) is indeed very appropriate to seize this real subject matter and expose it to the fullest. Lady Lou, a singer, in order to exchange her love for men's diamonds, spares no effort to show off her charm, causing many men to fall for her and be imprisoned for her crimes. Regarding this matter, many enthusiastic audiences will inevitably scold her as a "heartless妖婦", but the "love trade" in modern society will not be eliminated by this scolding. On the contrary, if we can gain some reflection, we should also give credit to this film. However, should we completely agree with the entire plot? No, when Detective Cummings led the police to arrest all these "villains", the detective finally fell in love with the dancer's beauty and released her out of love, even to the point of getting married and living together, which is very vulgar and unreasonable. Of course, we don't have to say that all sins should be attributed to this singer alone, but that the evil society made her and him commit crimes, but in terms of the plot itself, in order to make the plot quite reasonable, this singer should be brought to justice and punished. Moreover, from the point of view of "maintaining the spirit of the rule of law," how can this murderer escape justice? But the only explanation is that "she also worked hard for local public welfare," which precisely exposes the contradictions of capitalist films. Secondly, American movies still have to maintain the old tune of "lovers getting married."

As for the performance skills of this film, what I am most satisfied with is the success of the performance. Indeed, the heroine Mae West fully grasped the characteristics of this typical woman. She is so generous, and she is so calm in times of crisis, fully displaying her own dignity. She directs men to fight for her with extremely subtle movements. She seduces with sensuality, she fascinates with sound and color, but she is not exaggerated at all, completely removing the vulgar performance methods of "lust" and "heat." As for her singing voice, it is also very peculiar and moving. If, as the advertisement says, this is still her debut work, then we believe that she will definitely be a very promising "花且" in the future.

However, the success of the heroine is of course due to the director's efforts. In this film, we can see the director's exquisite techniques. He believes that music can help express emotions, so he accompanies the melodious love words with extremely low music. The heroine shines in the glittering golden jewelry and singing, fully expressing the golden beauty. Other small actions of the actors can also show the director's meticulousness. However, there are no particularly commendable shots in the entire film, and it is not successful in terms of mood, which is inevitably a lack.

I don't want to say much about other points. Anyway, they are all above the standard. In short, in terms of skills, this film is very satisfying.

Audience Opinions

Review of "New Year's Eve" 247

— Du Cunjie

Liu Jiqun and Chen Yanyan's Performances are Realistic

The Lianhua Film Company's newly produced "New Year's Eve" has been hyped for a long time, and finally premiered in "Beijing" today. After watching it, I think it is not bad, and there is nothing disappointing. Its story is based on tragedy as the background, depicting the morbidity of the times and the one-sidedness of urban social life. It can be called a tearful smile that satirizes the reality of life.

Its consciousness is very good; the three leading actors, Liu Jiqun, Chen Yanyan, and Jiang Junchao are also good. Especially Liu Jiqun and Chen Yanyan's expressions are very realistic, but the directing is a little bit imperfect; for example, in the scene when the old man asked and realized that it was the money for pawning his daughter, he couldn't help but jump up... At this point, Ms. Huang Yunzhen, who plays the old man's wife, her expression at the time only said that her daughter was willing to pawn herself to the third sister-in-law in exchange for money. Anyway, her daughter will always follow someone when she grows up. At this time, she doesn't have much sadness or resentment, since she is talking about her own flesh and blood, then this seems a bit unreasonable. The rest is pretty good. Overall, this film does not disappoint people.

Review of Dancing in "New Year's Eve" 248

— Gong Mengxuan

The dance scene interspersed in the middle of "New Year's Eve" is inevitably a bit far-fetched in terms of plot. Imagine that in this short period of time, a woman with unstable emotions is forced to learn to dance. No matter how easy dancing is, in fact, she will never learn the basic movements two or three times and be able to accompany the dance. An even more obvious loophole is that she has already made a lot of jokes about stepping on feet and bumping into people in public, and there are still many dancers rushing to ask her to accompany the dance!

In short, I think the director failed in "New Year's Eve." This is not because of a few small loopholes, but because he did not have a strict analysis of the personality of each character, which is the biggest reason for his failure.

The White Sister (3) 249

— Si Ping

Produced by MGM, Starring Helen Hayes

Sacrificing Reputation and Happiness for Love

Mina suddenly let out a cry, saying that her handbag had been snatched by a person standing next to her. Please Angela wait here, she went breathlessly to chase that person in the crowded crowd. Giovani took the opportunity to test whether Angela needed his help. She felt a little scared and a little unhappy about this behavior, so she twisted her eyebrow and only said, "Whatever you want." This slender soldier frankly said that he didn't want to go out, but wanted to talk to her.

"Oh!" His face flushed. "You should help. An old woman's purse has been stolen."

"I'll go find her. Please wait here. This is a whistle." He took it off from the rope circle around his neck. "If you're scared, you can blow it," he said, and rushed into the crowd. He stood on a square for a while, looking around blankly. In the sea of ​​merrymakers, he couldn't see the fat old woman, so he hurriedly ran back.

Angela sat at a table placed by the roadside of a small cafe. The melodious violin music came from the cafe.

"I can't find her," Giovani said. "You better wait here. I'm afraid everyone won't be able to find you if you leave. Why don't we go into the cafe? We can have some tea. Don't you trust me?"

"Just... father," she hesitated. "What if he finds out..."

"Are you very afraid of him?" the man asked.

"I love him very much!" she said, following Giovani into the cafe. "Is your surname郎杜?" She asked shyly as he dragged a chair for her to sit down and ordered tea.

"Who is he?" the man's eyes searched her beautiful eyes.

"Oh... he's just... a friend of my friend. You know, he wears black boots and rides a white horse. Is it a coincidence? He is very moving."

"Very moving," Giovani's eyes shot into her eyes in agreement. "You are very moving!" Angela heard this and stood up to leave. Giovani offered a shy retention, and she sat down again. The soft violin music filled the air. The waiter brought the tea. Giovani laughed and talked, and Angela listened silently, his eyes shining with new brilliance, and her heart beating happily.

"What happened later?" she asked urgently as soon as he stopped.

"Later I joined the army."

"Yes... I saw a soldier." Angela looked down at the tea leaves at the bottom of her teacup.

"Did he fall in love?" Giovani asked urgently. (To be continued)
